Rasa Light Regular (Rasa-Light.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Rasa' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Light' = NID 1 'Rasa Light'.

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.

, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Rasa-Regular', Everything looks good.

Rasa Medium Regular (Rasa-Medium.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Rasa' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Medium' = NID 1 'Rasa Medium'.

Rasa SemiBold Regular (Rasa-SemiBold.ttf)

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Rasa-SemiBold', Everything looks good.

Rasa SemiBold Regular (Rasa-SemiBold.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Rasa-SemiBold', Everything looks good.

Rasa SemiBold Regular (Rasa-SemiBold.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Rasa' + 'Space' + NID 17 'SemiBold' = NID 1 'Rasa SemiBold'.

Mac NID 6

NID 6 is 'Rasa-Bold', Everything looks good.

Underline Position and Thickness

Underline Position and Thickness

Pass

Rasa Light Regular (Rasa-Light.ttf)

post

underline position and thickness

underlinePosition should be a negative and underlineThickness not 0 or negative.

underlinePosition is '-220'.
underlineThicknes is '90'.

Pass

Rasa Regular (Rasa-Regular.ttf)

post

underline position and thickness

underlinePosition should be a negative and underlineThickness not 0 or negative.

underlinePosition is '-213'.
underlineThicknes is '105'.

Pass

Rasa Medium Regular (Rasa-Medium.ttf)

post

underline position and thickness

underlinePosition should be a negative and underlineThickness not 0 or negative.
